style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The third quarter was the highest revenue in the company's history, overall results demonstrate solid financial growth as we approach the end of this year.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font Operating income for the third quarter was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$4.5B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$1.0B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">30%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;from a year ago. The company generated </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$3.3B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net income for the third quarter, up </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">12%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;from a year ago.  Earnings per share was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">66</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;cents, up </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">14%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;from a year ago. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Third quarter gross margin of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">65%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was up half a point from the second quarter and down one point from our guidance. The increase from the second quarter was primarily due to lower platform* unit costs on 22nm and higher platform* volumes, mostly offset by higher production costs on 14nm products.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Our net inventory levels rose modestly quarter over quarter as we are efficiently managing capacity while ramping Broadwell on 14nm.&#160; The worldwide PC supply chain appears to be healthy, with inventory levels appropriate in anticipation of the fourth quarter retail cycles.  In the third quarter, we also repurchased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$4.2B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of stock.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">As we look forward to the fourth quarter of 2014, we are forecasting the midpoint of the revenue range at </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$14.7B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">up</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;from the third quarter. This forecast is in line with the historical average seasonal increase for the fourth quarter. We are forecasting the midpoint of the gross margin range for the fourth quarter to be </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">64%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The one point decrease from the third quarter is driven by higher platform* unit costs, higher factory start-up costs, partially offset by lower production costs on 14nm. </font></div><div The increase is driven by expected gains on sale of equity investments in the fourth quarter.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font
